\begin{isamarkuptext}%
From now on, there are two possible models for \isa{num}: as positive
  naturals (rule \isa{num{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}induct}) and as digit representation (rules
  \isa{num{\isachardot}{\kern0pt}induct}, \isa{num{\isachardot}{\kern0pt}cases}).%
\end{isamarkuptext}\isamarkuptrue%
%

\begin{isamarkuptext}%
The \isa{eq{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}numeral{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}iff{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}iszero} lemmas are not declared \isa{{\isacharbrackleft}{\kern0pt}simp{\isacharbrackright}{\kern0pt}} by default,
  because for rings of characteristic zero, better simp rules are possible.
  For a type like integers mod \isa{n}, type-instantiated versions of these rules
  should be added to the simplifier, along with a type-specific rule for
  deciding propositions of the form \isa{iszero\ {\isacharparenleft}{\kern0pt}numeral\ w{\isacharparenright}{\kern0pt}}.

  bh: Maybe it would not be so bad to just declare these as simp rules anyway?
  I should test whether these rules take precedence over the \isa{ring{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}char{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}{\isadigit{0}}}
  rules in the simplifier.%
\end{isamarkuptext}\isamarkuptrue%
\isacommand{lemma}\isamarkupfalse%
\ eq{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}numeral{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}iff{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}iszero{\isacharcolon}{\kern0pt}\isanewline
\ \ {\isachardoublequoteopen}numeral\ x\ {\isacharequal}{\kern0pt}\ numeral\ y\ {\isasymlongleftrightarrow}\ iszero\ {\isacharparenleft}{\kern0pt}sub\ x\ y{\isacharparenright}{\kern0pt}{\isachardoublequoteclose}\isanewline
\ \ {\isachardoublequoteopen}numeral\ x\ {\isacharequal}{\kern0pt}\ {\isacharminus}{\kern0pt}\ numeral\ y\ {\isasymlongleftrightarrow}\ iszero\ {\isacharparenleft}{\kern0pt}numeral\ {\isacharparenleft}{\kern0pt}x\ {\isacharplus}{\kern0pt}\ y{\isacharparenright}{\kern0pt}{\isacharparenright}{\kern0pt}{\isachardoublequoteclose}\isanewline
\ \ {\isachardoublequoteopen}{\isacharminus}{\kern0pt}\ numeral\ x\ {\isacharequal}{\kern0pt}\ numeral\ y\ {\isasymlongleftrightarrow}\ iszero\ {\isacharparenleft}{\kern0pt}numeral\ {\isacharparenleft}{\kern0pt}x\ {\isacharplus}{\kern0pt}\ y{\isacharparenright}{\kern0pt}{\isacharparenright}{\kern0pt}{\isachardoublequoteclose}\isanewline
\ \ {\isachardoublequoteopen}{\isacharminus}{\kern0pt}\ numeral\ x\ {\isacharequal}{\kern0pt}\ {\isacharminus}{\kern0pt}\ numeral\ y\ {\isasymlongleftrightarrow}\ iszero\ {\isacharparenleft}{\kern0pt}sub\ y\ x{\isacharparenright}{\kern0pt}{\isachardoublequoteclose}\isanewline
\ \ {\isachardoublequoteopen}numeral\ x\ {\isacharequal}{\kern0pt}\ {\isadigit{1}}\ {\isasymlongleftrightarrow}\ iszero\ {\isacharparenleft}{\kern0pt}sub\ x\ One{\isacharparenright}{\kern0pt}{\isachardoublequoteclose}\isanewline
\ \ {\isachardoublequoteopen}{\isadigit{1}}\ {\isacharequal}{\kern0pt}\ numeral\ y\ {\isasymlongleftrightarrow}\ iszero\ {\isacharparenleft}{\kern0pt}sub\ One\ y{\isacharparenright}{\kern0pt}{\isachardoublequoteclose}\isanewline
\ \ {\isachardoublequoteopen}{\isacharminus}{\kern0pt}\ numeral\ x\ {\isacharequal}{\kern0pt}\ {\isadigit{1}}\ {\isasymlongleftrightarrow}\ iszero\ {\isacharparenleft}{\kern0pt}numeral\ {\isacharparenleft}{\kern0pt}x\ {\isacharplus}{\kern0pt}\ One{\isacharparenright}{\kern0pt}{\isacharparenright}{\kern0pt}{\isachardoublequoteclose}\isanewline
\ \ {\isachardoublequoteopen}{\isadigit{1}}\ {\isacharequal}{\kern0pt}\ {\isacharminus}{\kern0pt}\ numeral\ y\ {\isasymlongleftrightarrow}\ iszero\ {\isacharparenleft}{\kern0pt}numeral\ {\isacharparenleft}{\kern0pt}One\ {\isacharplus}{\kern0pt}\ y{\isacharparenright}{\kern0pt}{\isacharparenright}{\kern0pt}{\isachardoublequoteclose}\isanewline
\ \ {\isachardoublequoteopen}numeral\ x\ {\isacharequal}{\kern0pt}\ {\isadigit{0}}\ {\isasymlongleftrightarrow}\ iszero\ {\isacharparenleft}{\kern0pt}numeral\ x{\isacharparenright}{\kern0pt}{\isachardoublequoteclose}\isanewline
\ \ {\isachardoublequoteopen}{\isadigit{0}}\ {\isacharequal}{\kern0pt}\ numeral\ y\ {\isasymlongleftrightarrow}\ iszero\ {\isacharparenleft}{\kern0pt}numeral\ y{\isacharparenright}{\kern0pt}{\isachardoublequoteclose}\isanewline
\ \ {\isachardoublequoteopen}{\isacharminus}{\kern0pt}\ numeral\ x\ {\isacharequal}{\kern0pt}\ {\isadigit{0}}\ {\isasymlongleftrightarrow}\ iszero\ {\isacharparenleft}{\kern0pt}numeral\ x{\isacharparenright}{\kern0pt}{\isachardoublequoteclose}\isanewline
\ \ {\isachardoublequoteopen}{\isadigit{0}}\ {\isacharequal}{\kern0pt}\ {\isacharminus}{\kern0pt}\ numeral\ y\ {\isasymlongleftrightarrow}\ iszero\ {\isacharparenleft}{\kern0pt}numeral\ y{\isacharparenright}{\kern0pt}{\isachardoublequoteclose}\isanewline

\isamarkupsubsubsection{Special Simplification for Constants%
}
\isamarkuptrue%
%
\endisatagdocument
{\isafolddocument}%

\isadelimdocument
%
\endisadelimdocument
%
\begin{isamarkuptext}%
These distributive laws move literals inside sums and differences.%
\end{isamarkuptext}\isamarkuptrue%
\isacommand{lemmas}\isamarkupfalse%

\isacommand{lemmas}\isamarkupfalse%
\ right{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}diff{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}distrib{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}numeral\ {\isacharbrackleft}{\kern0pt}simp{\isacharbrackright}{\kern0pt}\ {\isacharequal}{\kern0pt}\ right{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}diff{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}distrib\ {\isacharbrackleft}{\kern0pt}of\ {\isachardoublequoteopen}numeral\ v{\isachardoublequoteclose}{\isacharbrackright}{\kern0pt}\ \isakeyword{for}\ v%
\begin{isamarkuptext}%
These are actually for fields, like real%
\end{isamarkuptext}\isamarkuptrue%
